\doxysubsection*{Typedefs}
\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
using \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} = \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}(1, 3)+\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}(3, 1) \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac3184a4056593db0d92e28fe3684dc31}{results}} in \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}=1. 2. 3. 4. 5. 6. 7. 8. 10. Addition, subtraction and multiplication of \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a8108d1da2c3f0356a60d03af47f7c055}{matrices}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} denoted \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}}+, -\/, and $\ast$. The \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a97607d1b57ca47c9c7fdb29a25fad589}{operations}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} performed whenever \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a8108d1da2c3f0356a60d03af47f7c055}{matrices}} have \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} proper dimensions. For \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a0a6783062f9a26ee120e37823d63672a}{example}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a29faf1efa547eee7395013df5586bda5}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} above \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_ae849e958ef881cf7139efb79cce63618}{x}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} expressions \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}}+\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} incorrect because \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} 3 \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} 3 and \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} now 3 \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} 1. However, \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}=\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} correct and \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac3184a4056593db0d92e28fe3684dc31}{results}} in \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} output \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}=9.\+7248 17.\+6496 28.\+7159 Note that both upper and lower case \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_ac7b29261efa3c68c522873037cb2151f}{letters}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} allowed for input(on those \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac12c6f683435b156110d7c81beb90880}{systems}} which have both). There \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} two \char`\"{}matrix division\char`\"{} symbols in L\+A\+LA, \textbackslash{} and/. If \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a8108d1da2c3f0356a60d03af47f7c055}{matrices}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab997fb21bef012bb466f3fafefe8f35d}{then}} A\textbackslash{}B and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} correspond formally to left and right multiplication of \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} inverse of \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}}, that \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} inv(\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}}) $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} $\ast$inv(\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}}), but \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} result \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} obtained directly without \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} computation of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} inverse. In \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} scalar case, 3\textbackslash{}1 and 1/3 have \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} same \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a486541a7fdb4e2a6a51b1a062164ae74}{value}}, namely one-\/third. In general, A\textbackslash{}B denotes \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} solution \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} to \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} equation \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}}=\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} denotes \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} solution to \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}}=B. Left division, A\textbackslash{}B, \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} defined whenever \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} has \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac85e1322e210cd3e55055a318bee02d8}{as}} many rows \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac85e1322e210cd3e55055a318bee02d8}{as}} A. If \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} square, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ad6ef64fb9b12015a107b9ed4c99aac5b}{it}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} factored using Gaussian elimination. The factors \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} used to solve \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} equations \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}}(\+:, \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a7b867511ac48c9ebe39689231dfee9b2}{j}})=\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}(\+:, \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a7b867511ac48c9ebe39689231dfee9b2}{j}}) where \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}(\+:, \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a7b867511ac48c9ebe39689231dfee9b2}{j}}) denotes \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a7b867511ac48c9ebe39689231dfee9b2}{j}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_aa1b506237e40d77ec1834f07aee57310}{th}} column of B. The result \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a87f6540bdacc78d66aa258ba9cb8419a}{matrix}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a29faf1efa547eee7395013df5586bda5}{with}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} same \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_aea7cc0ff9e75deadea15b616599de8e6}{dimensions}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac85e1322e210cd3e55055a318bee02d8}{as}} B. If \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} nearly singular(according to \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} L\+I\+N\+P\+A\+CK condition estimator, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a4d930d019be5faa57dde81afc4ad296e}{R\+C\+O\+ND}}(3f)), \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} warning message \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} printed. If \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} not square, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ad6ef64fb9b12015a107b9ed4c99aac5b}{it}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} factored using Householder orthogonalization \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a29faf1efa547eee7395013df5586bda5}{with}} column pivoting. The factors \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} used to solve \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} under-\/ or overdetermined equations in \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} least squares sense. The result \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} an \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_aeaa87295020e1111fdb763522930f934}{M}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a4022e3ba0b80add8a3f7296344f89334}{N}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a87f6540bdacc78d66aa258ba9cb8419a}{matrix}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} where \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_aeaa87295020e1111fdb763522930f934}{M}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} number of columns of \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a4022e3ba0b80add8a3f7296344f89334}{N}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} number of columns of \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} . Each column of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} has at most \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a81a6880416ed81de652fd0cd1992ab06}{K}} nonzero components, where \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a81a6880416ed81de652fd0cd1992ab06}{K}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} effective rank of \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} . Right division, \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}}, can be defined in terms of left division \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}}=(\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}}\textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}}\textquotesingle{})\textquotesingle{}. For \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a0a6783062f9a26ee120e37823d63672a}{example}}, since our vector \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2c4bfc2c8ccb530ad950f7992d21ce6b}{b}} was \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a6d4e164739bb3d14a7e820f8236dcb0d}{computed}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac85e1322e210cd3e55055a318bee02d8}{as}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_ac3d69c76f758298bbad04b5f0f067d5a}{statement}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a98c7ccada846190eeea79403addb09be}{Y}}=A\textbackslash{}B \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac3184a4056593db0d92e28fe3684dc31}{results}} in \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a98c7ccada846190eeea79403addb09be}{Y}}=-\/1.\+3000 0.\+8000 3.\+1416 Of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a4ca86429c99a51a880c211ec3b9289b8}{course}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a98c7ccada846190eeea79403addb09be}{Y}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} not exactly \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a6bcb3e27afc22552106ea23d58ae10ab}{equal}} to \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} because of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} roundoff errors involved in both \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} and A\textbackslash{}B, but we \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} not \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_ac377b3442d374cf11bccfd1709172192}{printing}} enough digits to see \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} difference. The result of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_ac3d69c76f758298bbad04b5f0f067d5a}{statement}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a8415bf0d6f3303b94932caff6f017859}{E}}=\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} -\/ \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a98c7ccada846190eeea79403addb09be}{Y}} depends upon \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} particular \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2abbe4edf4ac16c700da1b1fddfb16ad}{computer}} being used. In one case \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ad6ef64fb9b12015a107b9ed4c99aac5b}{it}} produces \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a8415bf0d6f3303b94932caff6f017859}{E}}=1.\+0e-\/15 $\ast$.\+3053 -\/.\+2498 .\+0000 The quantity 1.\+0e-\/15 \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} scale \mbox{\hyperlink{mold_8f90_a9bbeeb28d89022ddb43927cf6638c6e3}{factor}} which multiplies all \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} components which follow. Thus our vectors \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a98c7ccada846190eeea79403addb09be}{Y}} actually agree to about 15 decimal places on this computer. It \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ade3819bf3b3e0fd29e1b0074f4990c96}{also}} possible to obtain element-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}}-\/element multiplicative operations. If \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} have \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} same \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_aea7cc0ff9e75deadea15b616599de8e6}{dimensions}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab997fb21bef012bb466f3fafefe8f35d}{then}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} .$\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} denotes \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a87f6540bdacc78d66aa258ba9cb8419a}{matrix}} whose elements \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} simply \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} products of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} individual elements of \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} . The expressions \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} ./\mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} .\textbackslash{} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a5a1a457b0aab366bdd0f5d93ffbb02f7}{B}} give \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} quotients of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} individual elements. There \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ae2fdc33bcd49731e36913fa7258b0dc8}{are}} several possible output formats. The \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_ac3d69c76f758298bbad04b5f0f067d5a}{statement}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a6a57e169570e057e93e4b2f0038ea255}{long}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ac3184a4056593db0d92e28fe3684dc31}{results}} in \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_af536e6b6e19b0639461fca9bcd715b9c}{X}}=-\/1.\+300000000000000 .\+800000000000000 3.\+141592653589793 The \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_ac3d69c76f758298bbad04b5f0f067d5a}{statement}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_a07e255a0fba822e24cedf6105ff270c1}{short}} restores \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a7fa3434e865bb9ba2c248c40b6a4faa2}{original}} format. The \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ab058871c43dd3d7a0111189f937f3127}{expression}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} $\ast$$\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a299fe281a9836080894d14b572094b33}{p}} means \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} to \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a299fe281a9836080894d14b572094b33}{p}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_aa1b506237e40d77ec1834f07aee57310}{th}} power. It \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} defined if \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abdb34322ff76ea8e7365a03da7d4167e}{A}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} square \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a87f6540bdacc78d66aa258ba9cb8419a}{matrix}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a299fe281a9836080894d14b572094b33}{p}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a19cefbe49a077540b7e33d4204e4b952}{a}} scalar. If \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a299fe281a9836080894d14b572094b33}{p}} \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} an integer greater \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a4602821dafb9f6eeb17c6c1a12f02d2c}{than}} one, \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} power \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_abf86c805fff53b12fdd4129aff834228}{is}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a6d4e164739bb3d14a7e820f8236dcb0d}{computed}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a40eab2bd454e9f761f2d13dffa13fb19}{by}} repeated multiplication. For other values of \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a299fe281a9836080894d14b572094b33}{p}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} calculation involves \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_a2857bbd4b5d07a07f178c59b854d9c80}{the}} \mbox{\hyperlink{test1_8txt_ad5f99263093734c58068b49554244f83}{eigenvalues}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{manual_8txt_ad1e7ecbfa7ed148b0078e2603c5cbcb9}{eigenvectors}} of A.
